< text>
Is it possible to give 10 stars? I have significant back and neck injuries related to college and high school football that had become reaggravated to the point it was unbearable. I called Synapse for an emergency adjustment as a new patient and was set-up with an appointment same day which actually cut into their lunch closure hour to accommodate me. Their clinic is spotless and brand new & extremely clean. I was greeted immediately at the door and given a tour of the operations. As a new patient I received their initial consult special which included a posture analysis, temperature scan of my spine, and muscle scan along with x-rays of areas that had been of issue- all of which is done in-house! After this process, which was incredible efficient, I met with Dr. Sahota and Dr. Todd who both handled aspects of my issues and their approach to wellness plan. I then received an adjustment and within a few hours of completion I had full range of motion back in my neck with no pain for the first time in over a month and had some relief in my lower back as well. Later that evening I received a call at home checking on my status from Dr. Todd direct & this morning I got a text with a personalized detail of my follow-up appointment that is set. It is rare in this day and age to receive good service and care & generally it is only one aspect of the process. The Synapse Team is truly 10 star and did everything possible to show me my wellness mattered to them. I have made two referrals already this morning and there will be many more to follow. As a college football player at a Division 1 School I received great medical attention but this has been by far the best overall experience I have had anywhere with great results. I am excited again for the thought of a future that might include a back and neck that are pain free.< /text>

To me, it is Don Cuco's or Olvera St. if you want good Mexican food.<//Text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMD5lWIiqcNyf2gs_pDsJAH7ax6TlziQzz-U4s=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMigwxsCdEyD0d0_3DpHzeW9_BIrPwgKDs3TEY=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN5IVtOAR5VqcrY1tRWlHtL0lJwBRSG35VxGMs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics>< Response>

<resp>None<//resp><Review>As we sat outside and ate at a restaurant for the first time in what seemed years,  Don Cuco made this a pleasant experience.

The greeters and waiters made sure to cater to all customers quickly and attentively. The food came out steaming hot. The frozen Cadillac margaritas I ordered possessed a good amount of liquor. Lastly, they made sure our drinks were topped off.

The Surf and Turf burrito is a must here. The black beans and chicken soup made this a favorite of mines.

The Quesadilla Santa Fe was great, but the only problem I had with is would be attributed to the dryness on the fringes. It needed a little help with some salsa on the ends and needs a little more cheese to help keep it together.

If you're in the area and they have room on the patio, check them out!<//Review>< Gmap_id>

< Review>
Very fun Mexican restaurant!  Come for the atmosphere, location, and drinks but not the food. The food is above average but not the best.  I would categorize it as greasy Mexican food vs light Mexican food.  They do have a large menu, so if you are looking to eat healthy, you can definitely find something.  I still give this place five starts because the service has always been great.  We have a work Thanksgiving party at the Riverside location that gets bigger and bigger every year.  The restaurant is always happy to have us, is very accommodating, our food always comes in a timely manner, and the drinks are always on point.  I‚Äôm not a big margarita drinker, but my co-workers have always complemented the Cadillac Margarita.    This location is always busy but never crowded enough that it prevents me from recommending to others or having meetups.  The clientele is very chill, mostly being frequented by the surrounded businesses and studio employees.  The bar is somewhat narrow so if you plan on eating, think about getting a table or booth to give yourself a little more space.  Great restaurant filled with lots of great memories! üëç</Review>

< Review>
The atmosphere was great, the service was great. Free Chips & Salsa can't go wrong with that. Now let's dive in; ever since I've been watching nightmares kitchen I critique restaurants differently. The salsa tasted it like it came from a can which is probably why it's free. The margarita was $10 however it had artificial flavoring and it wasn't craft. The margarita is definitely not worth the price which turned me off. The only time I would go back to this restaurant is if it's on somebody else's dime, so then I don't feel bad for having mediocre salsa and drinks. If you're looking for a place that serves great food and great drinks this is not your place but if you're looking for a place to Hangout and not really concerned with the drinks or food check this spot out.< /Review>

< text>
Good, standard Mexican food, well-made, generous margueritas, and really excellent, attentive service. It's not cutting edge fancy-mex, but, when you want good, standard Mexican in the Burbank area, in a pleasant, buzzing, low-light atmosphere, it's a good choice. Prices, moderate, in the 20's for an entre, which comes with soup or salad. The albondogas cup was tasty, but just one meatball. The combo plates are generous, you are unlikely to leave hungry.< /text>

<user_name>Karen Farmiloe< /user_name>< Date>
1521240389183<//Date>
< rating>
4< /rating>
< review>
I grew up in Burbank so this place was a staple growing up. I have since moved away, but do try to go anytime I am back in town. This past Sunday I did just that! There are many Don Cuco's around the southland, but this one is the original. Although I have not been to each location, I have been to many of them. I believe this one is the best for atmosphere, stargazing (its close to the studios so you never know who you may run in to) and food quality. I also think their margarita's are better at this location. The service is good and the servers are super nice. I normally just get a bean and cheese burrito, but today I got the El Taco Grande with Albondigas soup. It kinda reminded me of the Taco Light from Taco Bell years ago, but much better! The soup was very good! My husband got the Lobster Enchiladas. He didn't LOVE them, but he did like them. He believes it was probably more Langostino meat than Lobster meat. He didn't ask to confirm so he could be wrong. Nevertheless, he did enjoy them for the most part. The prices are decent, although I think this location is higher priced then the one in Newhall, Ca. I also believe the menu to be a little different.<//review>
